installation, Formlabs software may ask you to consent to the collection of diagnostic information regarding your use of Formlabs software or hardware in order to help our engineers improve Formlabs products. If you consent, you agree that Formlabs may collect, maintain, and use information about the operation of your Formlabs hardware and software, such as hardware serial numbers, print times, laser power levels, and 3D model sizes. No models, 3D geometry, or Personal Information will be collected without your additional and explicit consent.</p>
<p>If you choose to create an online account with the Dashboard or use a printer that has been previously connected to the Dashboard, you agree that Formlabs may collect, maintain, and use information about the operation of your Formlabs hardware and software, such as hardware serial numbers, print times, laser power levels, resin type and volume, temperature, 3D model size, and other information relevant to printer operation. Further, the Dashboard users agree to share an isometric view of 3D models to be used for preview purposes within the user interface. Full models, 3D geometry, and Personal Information will not be collected without your additional and explicit consent. By opting to use our “Remote Print” feature, you are consenting to share part print files with Formlabs. Formlabs will use these print files in accordance with this Privacy Policy in order to remotely upload your object to the designated printer through Dashboard. Formlabs may ask you to provide feedback regarding your printing experience. Any feedback will also be collected, maintained, and used by Formlabs in accordance with this Privacy Policy.</p>
<p>Information collected for and by the Dashboard will be associated with specific printers, identifiable by serial name. Users will access the printer through an encrypted MAC address where they will be prompted to create a username and password. Users who create an account will be able to associate printers with their account using the unique encrypted MAC address of the printer accessible via the printer’s user interface. Multiple user accounts may be associated with each printer, but each user must have physical access to the printer. Each user will be able to see every print job queued to the printer, but will be unable to associate print jobs with specific users unless the users self-identify in the print job’s title.</p></div></div><div class="section-5100383 Grid_section__Nq73A" id=""><style>@media (min-width:1024px){

This information is used by Formlabs for the operation of the Websites and Services, to maintain the quality of the Websites and Services, and to provide general statistics regarding use of the Websites and Services. This temporary storage of information by the system is necessary to allow the delivery of the Websites and Services to the user’s computer. In addition, this information is used to optimize the Websites and Services and to ensure the security of our information technology systems. This information is not used for marketing purposes. Header_theme__tkmrI">Rights of California Consumers</h3></span><span class="AlignmentWrapper_content__Aq_1_"><div class="text-plugin" style='type:"../atoms/Type/typography.css";paragraph-weight:400;paragraph-large:1.125rem;paragraph-large-lh:1.75rem;paragraph-medium:1rem;paragraph-medium-lh:1.55rem;paragraph-small:.875rem;paragraph-small-lh:1.25rem;paragraph-xsmall:.75rem;paragraph-xsmall-lh:1.25rem;label-weight:600;label-large:1.125rem;label-large-lh:1.55rem;label-medium:1rem;label-medium-lh:1.25rem;label-small:.875rem;label-small-lh:1rem;label-xsmall:.75rem;label-xsmall-lh:1rem;display-large:6rem;display-large-tablet:4.5rem;display-large-mobile:2.625rem;display-large-lh:117%;display-medium:3.25rem;display-medium-mobile:2rem;display-medium-lh:123%;display-small:2.75rem;display-small-mobile:1.875rem;display-small-lh:118%;display-xsmall:2.25rem;display-xsmall-mobile:1.75rem;display-xsmall-lh:122%;display-weight:700;colors:"../../styles/colors.css";black700:#000000;white700:#FFFFFF;grey600:#333333;grey400:#63666A;grey300:#A4A6A8;grey200:#D0D0CE;grey100:#E0E0E0;grey50:#F3F3F3;no-margins:TextPlugin_noMargins___EfdZ;p-xs:TextPlugin_p-xs__pw9En;p-sm:TextPlugin_p-sm__XoKrs;p-md:TextPlugin_p-md__poY3c;p-lg:TextPlugin_p-lg__TGqPI;l-xs:TextPlugin_l-xs__aaQ__;l-sm:TextPlugin_l-sm__to84b;l-md:TextPlugin_l-md__yFPU1;l-lg:TextPlugin_l-lg__7ZDrv;d-lg:TextPlugin_d-lg__54B4I;d-md:TextPlugin_d-md__JcN4C;d-sm:TextPlugin_d-sm__tYE66;d-xs:TextPlugin_d-xs__MvlgH;dark:TextPlugin_dark__A07Vr;theme:TextPlugin_theme__sG0yW;light:TextPlugin_light__HiOH1;light-primary:TextPlugin_light-primary__T9iQj;theme-primary:TextPlugin_theme-primary__3Eemr;light-secondary:TextPlugin_light-secondary__43OII;theme-secondary:TextPlugin_theme-secondary__0Azl_;light-tertiary:TextPlugin_light-tertiary__F_51K;theme-tertiary:TextPlugin_theme-tertiary__nl_Pb;dark-primary:TextPlugin_dark-primary__TRZY3;dark-secondary:TextPlugin_dark-secondary__Dqr1Y;dark-tertiary:TextPlugin_dark-tertiary__yOGRN;emphasis-primary:TextPlugin_emphasis-primary__SpdcD;emphasis:TextPlugin_emphasis__yfr5a;emphasis-secondary:TextPlugin_emphasis-secondary__rz0ck;emphasis-tertiary:TextPlugin_emphasis-tertiary__1gnWG'><p>As of January 1, 2020, California law permits residents of California to request certain details about how their Personal Information is shared. California residents may exercise the following rights with respect to their Personal Information: </p>
<p><strong>Access</strong></p>
<p>California consumers may request that Formlabs disclose to them the Personal Information Formlabs collects, uses, discloses, and sells, up to two times per year. Once we confirm your verifiable request, we will disclose your Personal Information we collect, use, disclose, and sell, if applicable.</p>
<p><strong>Deletion</strong></p>
<p>Consumers may request the deletion of their Personal Information collected or maintained by us. Once we confirm your verifiable request, we will delete your Personal Information from our records. We may deny your request for deletion where an exception exists. </p>
<p><strong>Other Rights</strong></p>
<p>In addition to the rights above, once per year California consumers may also request certain information about our disclosure of Personal Information to third parties for their own direct marketing purposes during the preceding calendar year. Subject to exception for incentives that are reasonably related to the value of Personal Information, California consumers also have the right not to be discriminated against for exercising any of the rights listed above.</p>
<p><strong>Exercising Your Rights and Verifying Your Request</strong></p>
<p>If you wish to exercise any of your CCPA rights, please contact us at <a class="__cf_email__" data-cfemail="cabab8a3bcaba9b38aaca5b8a7a6aba8b9e4a9a5a7e4" href="/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection">[email protected]</a> Formlabs will then reasonably verify your request by matching the identifying information you provide with your personal information maintained by Formlabs.</p></div></span></div></div></span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><nav aria-label="Page footer navigation" class="Footer_footer__IMsV7" role="contentinfo"><div
